    <script>

    function onLinkedTermSelected(session, data) {
      
        let cookieData = {
            return_url: document.URL,
            externalTermId: data.linkedTermData.externalTermId,
            sessionId: session
        };
        
        let newUrl = data.linkedTermData.subscriptionManagementUrl + '&PLTO=' + btoa(JSON.stringify(cookieData));
        
        window.open(newUrl, '_self');
        return false;
    }

    window.NWZ?.EventSystem?.subscribe("TrackPaywallClick", () => {

    function crawlWidgetsForArticleIds(data) {
        ids = [];
        if (typeof data === undefined) {
            return ids;
        }


            data.forEach(function(element) {
                targetContainer = document.querySelector('#' + element.widgetParams.targetElementId);
                if( typeof targetContainer.dataset.pianoExcludedIds != 'undefined' ) {
                    pianoExcludedContainerIds = targetContainer.dataset.pianoExcludedIds;
                    pianoExcludedContainerIds = pianoExcludedContainerIds.split(',');
                    pianoExcludedContainerIds.forEach(function(id) {
                        document.querySelectorAll('section[data-contentport-id="' + id + '"]').forEach(function(el) {
                            el.querySelectorAll('section[data-articleid]').forEach(function(a) {
                                if( a.dataset.articleid.length > 0 ) {
                                    ids.push(a.dataset.articleid);
                                }                            
                            })
                        })
                    })
                }
            });

        return ids
    }

    function showPianoMultiRecos(data = false) {
		widgets = [];
				
		if( Array.isArray(data) === false || typeof data === undefined ) {
			return false;
		} 
			
		data.forEach(function(element) {
			if( document.querySelector('#' + element.widgetParams.targetElementId) ) {
				widgets.push( element );
			}
        });
		
		if( Array.isArray(widgets) === false ) {
			return false;
		}

		cX.CCE.callQueue.push(['runMulti', widgets, true, crawlWidgetsForArticleIds(widgets)]);
	}

    function onRegWallDisplay() {
        WK.PianoComposer.disableDataLayerValues().onPaywallDisplay();
        console.log('Piano WK-RayWall - TS triggered via portal');
    }

    function onPaywallDisplayNWZ() {
        // See PianoComposer.ts
        NWZ.PianoComposer.onPaywallDisplay();
        console.log('Piano NWZ-Paywall - TS triggered via portal');
    }

    }

        <script id="showAds">
        const isStudiPlus = function() {
            if (NWZ.User.hasStudentSub())
                return true;

            const param = new URL(location).searchParams.get("abotypestudiplus");
            return param !== null && (param === "1" || param === "2" || param === "3" || param === "4" || param === "5")
        }
        const showAds = !isStudiPlus();
        </script>
        <script>
        const loadAdsFromJson = async function(key) {
                
            const response = await fetch("https://pageeditor.nwzonline.de/api/uploads/misc/campaigns.json");
            const jsonAds = await response.json();

            let campaigns = jsonAds[key]?.campaigns?.length || 0
            let randomCampaign = Math.floor(Math.random()*campaigns);

            const adConfig = jsonAds[key]?.campaigns[randomCampaign];
            
            if (!adConfig)
                return;

            const registerJsonAd = function(key, node) {
                const ad = adConfig?.creatives[key];
                if (!ad) {
                    node.remove();
                    return;
                }

                if (!isApp && typeof ad.html != "undefined" && ad.html != "") {
                    node.innerHTML = '<div class="fullsize"><iframe src="' + ad.html + '" frameborder="0" scrolling="no" width="' + ad.width + 'px" height="' + ad.height + 'px"></iframe></div>';
                }
                else if (typeof ad.path != "undefined" && ad.path != "") {
                    node.innerHTML = '<div class="fullsize"><a href="' + ad.url + '" target="_blank"><img src="' + ad.path + '" width="' + ad.width + 'px" height="' + ad.height + 'px"></a></div>';
                }
                else {
                    node.remove();
                }
            }

            if (Page.resolution.isDesktop) {
                registerJsonAd("banner", document.querySelector("#msn-ads-top"))
                registerJsonAd("sky", document.querySelector("#msn-ads-off-content-right-1"))
                registerJsonAd("rectangle", document.querySelector(".article-side .msn-ads"))
            }
            else {
                registerJsonAd("rectangle", document.querySelector(".article-body .msn-ads"))
            }
        }

        if (isStudiPlus()) {
            document.addEventListener("DOMContentLoaded", () => {
                document.querySelector("#msn-ads-out-of-page")?.remove();
                loadAdsFromJson("studiPlus")
            })
        }
    </script>

                adHandler.cmd.push(function() { 
                    const nwz_keywords = window.nwz_keywords || "";

                    const targeting = [
                        ["nwz_basetype", "site"],
                        ["nwz_type", "site"],

                        ["nwz_keywords", nwz_keywords],

                    ]

                    for (let t = 0; t < targeting.length; t++) {
                        adHandler.service.setTargeting(targeting[t][0], targeting[t][1])
                    }
                    adHandler.service.request();                   
                });

    <nav aria-label="Favoriten" class="fast-navi swipeable bg-white sticky z-7" style="display: none">

<script type="text/javascript">
function waitForElm(selector) {
    return new Promise(resolve => {
        if (document.querySelector(selector)) {
            return resolve(document.querySelector(selector));
        }

        const observer = new MutationObserver(mutations => {
            if (document.querySelector(selector)) {
                observer.disconnect();
                resolve(document.querySelector(selector));
            }
        });

        observer.observe(document.body, {
            childList: true,
            subtree: true
        });
    });
}

// possibly unused
waitForElm('#piano-target-rec3 .piano-reco-wrapper').then((elm) => {
    document.querySelectorAll('div[data-piano-template-class]').forEach(function(el) { 
        el.querySelector('section.piano-reco-wrapper.template').classList.remove('slot_3-col');
        el.querySelector('section.piano-reco-wrapper.template').classList.add(el.dataset.pianoTemplateClass);
        console.log('piano recos - switch template to: ' + el.dataset.pianoTemplateClass);
    });
    
});
</script>

            </h4>

            <section class="text fs:13 lh:2/3 ls:05 dyn-margin font-merriweather" style="--margin-top:0">
                    <p class="article-teaser">Am Mix-Markt-Parkplatz in Oldenburg drohen Autofahrern weiter Bußgelder – selbst, wenn sie gar nicht geparkt haben. Die Verbraucherzentrale hält viele Forderungen für unzulässig. Ein Fall landet nun vor Gericht.</p>

                </span>                
                Wenn Jugendliche Pornos gucken – So reagieren Eltern richtig
            </h4>

            <section class="text fs:13 lh:2/3 ls:05 dyn-margin font-merriweather" style="--margin-top:0">
                    <p class="article-teaser">Kinder sehen immer früher pornografische Inhalte, oft unfreiwillig. Beratende berichten von Überforderung und Angst. Fachleute fordern: Sexualität muss früh und offen besprochen werden. So gehen Eltern mit dem Thema um.</p>

                    ÖKOWERK EMDEN

                </span>                
                Eine „Mini-Achterbahn“ für Ostfrieslands ersten Baumwipfelpfad
            </h4>
        </header>

            <section class="text fs:13 lh:2/3 ls:05 dyn-margin font-merriweather" style="--margin-top:0">
                    <p class="article-teaser">Etagenweise das Ökosystem Wald erleben inklusive Aussicht „vom Dach“ – das machen Baumwipfelpfade möglich. Der erste Ostfrieslands nimmt gerade im Emder Ökowerk Gestalt an. Und zwar mächtig.</p>

                    "
                    >

                    WIRTSCHAFT

                </span>                
                Iran-Krise wird die Urlaubspläne vieler Deutscher verändern
            </h4>
        </header>

            <section class="text fs:13 lh:2/3 ls:05 dyn-margin font-merriweather" style="--margin-top:0">
                    <p class="article-teaser">Frieden als Voraussetzung für Tourismus – das betont die ITB in Berlin. Kriege und Krisen verändern die Reisepläne vieler Deutscher. Immer beliebter wird der Urlaub im eigenen Land – sicher, abwechslungsreich und ganz ohne Fernflug.</p>
            </section>


    </a>
